This Notification is made under sub-seclion (1) ofseclion 11 of the Right of Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement
Act,2013 (CentralAct 30 of2013), to allwhom it may concern.
A plan of the land may be inspecled in the oftice of the Collector and Land Acquisition Ofiicer on any working day during the working hours
The Govemment is pleased to authorize the requiring department i.e. Executive Engineer, VvRD \, Special Poect Division, Tirunelveli and his staff lo enter upon a
survey land, take levels of any lana, Jig o, Uore inlo ihe sib-soil and do all other acls reqlired for proper execution of their work as provided and specified in section 12
of the said Ac1.
under sub..section (4) of seclion 11 of the said Act, no person shall make any lransaction or cause any transaction of land ie. sale/purchase' etc or create any
encumbrances on such land from the date of publlcation of this notification in the faml Nadu G ovemment Gazette withoul prior approval of the Collec'tor.
Objections to lhe acquisition, if any, may be liled by the person interested within 60 (Sixty) days from the date of publication of this notification in the
Tamil Nidu Govemment Gazefte as ptovided under seclion 15 of the said Act before the Colleclor.

Act, 2013 (CenkalAcl 30 oI2013), to all whom it may concam.
A plan of the land may be inspected in ihe oflice ofthe Collector and Land Acquisition Officer on any working day during the working hours.
staff to enter upon a survey land, take levels of any land, dig or bore into the sub-soil and do all other acts required for the proper execution of their work as provid€d and
specified in seclion '12 of the said Act.
Under suFsection (4) of section 11 ofthe said Act, no person shall make any transaclion or cause any transaction ofland i.e. sale / purchase, etc or create any encumbrances
on such land from the daie of publication of this notilication in the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette without prior approval of the Collector.
Objec{ions to the acquisition, if any, may be filed by the person interested within 60 (Sixty ) days trom the date of publication ofthis notitication in the Tamil Nadu covernment
Gazette as provided under section 15 of the said Aci beforc the Collector

This notification is made under sub-section (1) of section 11 of the Right to Fair compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitaiion and Resettlement
Act, 2013 (CentralAct 30 of 2013), to all whom it may concern.
A plan ofthe land may be inspected in the office ofthe Collector and Land Acquisition Offcer on any working day during the working hours.
The Government is pleased to authorize the requiring department Executive Engineer, \A/ater Resources Department, Special Project Division' Tirunelveli and his staff
to enter upon a survey land, take levels of any land, dig or-bore into the sub-soil and d-o allolher acts required for the proper execution of their work as provided and specilied
in section 1 2 of the said Aci.
Under suFsection (4) of section 11 of the said Act, no person shall make any transaction or cause any transaclion of land i.e.,. sale/purchase' etc, or creale any
encumbrances on such land from lhs dals of public€tion of thi; notification in th a Tamil Nadu Gove,nment Gazette wilhout pdor aPproval of lhe collector.
Objeclions to lhe acquisition, if any, may be filed by the peBon interested wilhin 60 (Sixty) days trom the dale of publication of this notificalion in lhe Tamil Nadu
Gowrrment Gazene as prwided under Soction 15 of the said Act before the collec{or'

in Palayamkottai Taluk in Tirunelveli District for public purpose, namely Tamirabarani - Karumeniyar - Nambiyar lnterlinking Flood Carrier Canal Project. Environmental
lmpact Assessment study for the irigation project(i.e) Formation of llood carrier canal from Cannadian channel to Orought Prone Areas ot Sathankulam, Thisayanvilai by
interlinking Tamirabarani, Karumeniyar and Nambiyar rivers in Tirunelveli and Tuticorin Districts in Tamil Nadu has been carried out by 'WAPCOS' under the section 3(3) ofthe
Environmental Prolection Act, 1986. The land is acquired to wit for the formation of Flood Carrier Cananl. As the Environmental lmpact Assessment Study has been carried
out for this lrrigation Poect, Social lmpact Assessment shall not apply according to the provision of Sub Section 2(6) of Right to Fair Compensation, And Transparency
in Land Acquisition, Rehabiliiation and Resettlement Act, 2013 The Requisition body entered upon the project area on 12.11.2010 and canal was dug to Flood carrier
